000102e3 <simple_switch>:
// esp不用保存，只需要让esp保存在调用之前的状态

	.text
	.global simple_switch
simple_switch:

   102e3:	8b 44 24 04          	mov    0x4(%esp),%eax

   102eb:	55                   	push   %ebp
	push %ebx
   102ec:	53                   	push   %ebx
	push %esi
   102ed:	56                   	push   %esi
	push %edi
   102ee:	57                   	push   %edi

	// 切换栈
	mov %esp, (%eax)    // from->stack = esp
   102ef:	89 20                	mov    %esp,(%eax)
  	mov %edx, %esp      // esp = to->stack
   102f1:	89 d4                	mov    %edx,%esp

	pop %esi

	pop %ebx

  	ret

00010347 <write_cr3>:
	uint32_t cr2;

/**

 */
static uint32_t total_mem_size(boot_info_t * boot_info) {

    for (int i = 0; i < boot_info->ram_region_count; i++) {

   10593:	eb 16                	jmp    105ab <total_mem_size+0x2c>

   105a2:	01 d0                	add    %edx,%eax

pte_t * find_pte (pde_t * page_dir, uint32_t vaddr, int alloc) {

   105bc:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   105be:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
    pte_t * page_table;

   105c4:	e8 8a fd ff ff       	call   10353 <pde_index>
   105c9:	83 c4 04             	add    $0x4,%esp

   105de:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   105e1:	83 e0 01             	and    $0x1,%eax
   105e4:	84 c0                	test   %al,%al
   105e6:	74 10                	je     105f8 <find_pte+0x3d>

    } else {
        // 如果不存在，则考虑分配一个
        if (alloc == 0) {

   105fc:	75 07                	jne    10605 <find_pte+0x4a>
            return (pte_t *)0;
   105fe:	b8 00 00 00 00       	mov    $0x0,%eax
   10603:	eb 64                	jmp    10669 <find_pte+0xae>

   10625:	eb 42                	jmp    10669 <find_pte+0xae>

        // 清空页表，防止出现异常

   119fc:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)

static inline uint8_t inb(uint16_t  port) {

   1313b:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   1313d:	83 ec 14             	sub    $0x14,%esp
   13140:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   13143:	66 89 45 ec          	mov    %ax,-0x14(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("inb %[p], %[v]" : [v]"=a" (rv) : [p]"d"(port));
   13147:	0f b7 45 ec          	movzwl -0x14(%ebp),%eax
   1314b:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   1314d:	ec                   	in     (%dx),%al
   1314e:	88 45 ff             	mov    %al,-0x1(%ebp)
	return rv;
   13151:	0f b6 45 ff          	movzbl -0x1(%ebp),%eax
}

0001337b <console_select>:


void console_select(int idx) {
   1337b:	55                   	push   %ebp
   1337c:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   1337e:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
    console_t * console = console_buf + idx;
   13381:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax

   13387:	05 00 56 03 00       	add    $0x35600,%eax
   1338c:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)
    if (console->disp_base == 0) {   // 判断待切换的console是否完成初始化，即是否打开
   1338f:	8b 45 f4             	mov    -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   13392:	8b 00                	mov    (%eax),%eax
   13394:	85 c0                	test   %eax,%eax
   13396:	75 0e                	jne    133a6 <console_select+0x2b>
        // 可能没有初始化，先初始化一下
        console_init(idx);
   13398:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   1339b:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   1339e:	e8 9e 04 00 00       	call   13841 <console_init>
   133a3:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp

    // 计算console显存的起始位置
	uint16_t pos = idx * console->display_cols * console->display_rows;

   133a9:	8b 40 14             	mov    0x14(%eax),%eax
   133ac:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx

   133b1:	0f af d0             	imul   %eax,%edx

   133b7:	8b 40 10             	mov    0x10(%eax),%eax
   133ba:	0f af c2             	imul   %edx,%eax
   133bd:	66 89 45 f2          	mov    %ax,-0xe(%ebp)

	outb(0x3D4, 0xC);		// 向端口0x3D4写入0xC，表示下一步在往0x3D5端口写数据时写的是高8位位置数据，即16位地址的高8位
   133c1:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp

00013792 <move_next_tab>:

/**
 * 将光标对齐到8的倍数位置上
 */
static void move_next_tab(console_t * console) {
   13792:	55                   	push   %ebp
   13793:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   13795:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
    int col = console->cursor_col;
   13798:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   1379b:	8b 40 0c             	mov    0xc(%eax),%eax
   1379e:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)

    col = (col + 7) / 8 * 8;		// 下一显示位置
   137a1:	8b 45 f4             	mov    -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   137a4:	83 c0 07             	add    $0x7,%eax
   137a7:	8d 50 07             	lea    0x7(%eax),%edx
   137aa:	85 c0                	test   %eax,%eax
   137ac:	0f 48 c2             	cmovs  %edx,%eax
   137af:	c1 f8 03             	sar    $0x3,%eax
   137b2:	c1 e0 03             	shl    $0x3,%eax
   137b5:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)
    if (col >= console->display_cols) {
   137b8:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137bb:	8b 40 14             	mov    0x14(%eax),%eax
   137be:	39 45 f4             	cmp    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)
   137c1:	7c 36                	jl     137f9 <move_next_tab+0x67>
        col = 0;
   137c3:	c7 45 f4 00 00 00 00 	movl   $0x0,-0xc(%ebp)
        console->cursor_row++;
   137ca:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137cd:	8b 40 08             	mov    0x8(%eax),%eax
   137d0:	8d 50 01             	lea    0x1(%eax),%edx
   137d3:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137d6:	89 50 08             	mov    %edx,0x8(%eax)
        if (console->cursor_row >= console->display_rows) {
   137d9:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137dc:	8b 50 08             	mov    0x8(%eax),%edx
   137df:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137e2:	8b 40 10             	mov    0x10(%eax),%eax
   137e5:	39 c2                	cmp    %eax,%edx
   137e7:	7c 10                	jl     137f9 <move_next_tab+0x67>
            // 超出末端，上移
            scroll_up(console, 1);
   137e9:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp
   137ec:	6a 01                	push   $0x1
   137ee:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   137f1:	e8 c5 fc ff ff       	call   134bb <scroll_up>
   137f6:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
        }
    }
    console->cursor_col = col;
   137f9:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   137fc:	8b 55 f4             	mov    -0xc(%ebp),%edx
   137ff:	89 50 0c             	mov    %edx,0xc(%eax)
}

/**
 * 普通状态下的字符的写入处理
 */
static void write_normal (console_t * console, char c) {
   13962:	55                   	push   %ebp
   13963:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   13965:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
   13968:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   1396b:	88 45 f4             	mov    %al,-0xc(%ebp)
    switch (c) {
   1396e:	0f be 45 f4          	movsbl -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   13972:	83 f8 0a             	cmp    $0xa,%eax
   13975:	74 70                	je     139e7 <write_normal+0x85>
   13977:	83 f8 0a             	cmp    $0xa,%eax
   1397a:	7f 0c                	jg     13988 <write_normal+0x26>
   1397c:	83 f8 08             	cmp    $0x8,%eax
   1397f:	74 34                	je     139b5 <write_normal+0x53>
   13981:	83 f8 09             	cmp    $0x9,%eax
   13984:	74 41                	je     139c7 <write_normal+0x65>
   13986:	eb 6f                	jmp    139f7 <write_normal+0x95>
   13988:	83 f8 1b             	cmp    $0x1b,%eax
   1398b:	74 0c                	je     13999 <write_normal+0x37>
   1398d:	83 f8 7f             	cmp    $0x7f,%eax
   13990:	74 13                	je     139a5 <write_normal+0x43>
   13992:	83 f8 0d             	cmp    $0xd,%eax
   13995:	74 40                	je     139d7 <write_normal+0x75>
   13997:	eb 5e                	jmp    139f7 <write_normal+0x95>
        case ASCII_ESC:
            console->write_state = CONSOLE_WRITE_ESC;
   13999:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   1399c:	c7 40 04 01 00 00 00 	movl   $0x1,0x4(%eax)
            break;
   139a3:	eb 72                	jmp    13a17 <write_normal+0xb5>
        case 0x7F:
            erase_backword(console);
   139a5:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   139a8:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   139ab:	e8 78 ff ff ff       	call   13928 <erase_backword>
   139b0:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
            break;
   139b3:	eb 62                	jmp    13a17 <write_normal+0xb5>
        case '\b':		// 左移一个字符
            move_backword(console, 1);

            // 换行处理

00013a43 <write_esc>:

/**
 * 写入以ESC开头的序列
 */
static void write_esc (console_t * console, char c) {
   13a43:	55                   	push   %ebp
   13a44:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   13a46:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
   13a49:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   13a4c:	88 45 f4             	mov    %al,-0xc(%ebp)
    // https://blog.csdn.net/ScilogyHunter/article/details/106874395
    // ESC状态处理, 转义序列模式 ESC 0x20-0x27(0或多个) 0x30-0x7e
    switch (c) {
   13a4f:	0f be 45 f4          	movsbl -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   13a53:	83 f8 38             	cmp    $0x38,%eax
   13a56:	74 21                	je     13a79 <write_esc+0x36>
   13a58:	83 f8 5b             	cmp    $0x5b,%eax
   13a5b:	74 33                	je     13a90 <write_esc+0x4d>
   13a5d:	83 f8 37             	cmp    $0x37,%eax
   13a60:	75 48                	jne    13aaa <write_esc+0x67>
        case '7':		// ESC 7 保存光标
            save_cursor(console);
   13a62:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   13a65:	e8 9b fd ff ff       	call   13805 <save_cursor>
   13a6a:	83 c4 04             	add    $0x4,%esp

0001413a <inb>:
static inline uint8_t inb(uint16_t  port) {
   1413a:	55                   	push   %ebp
   1413b:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   1413d:	83 ec 14             	sub    $0x14,%esp
   14140:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   14143:	66 89 45 ec          	mov    %ax,-0x14(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("inb %[p], %[v]" : [v]"=a" (rv) : [p]"d"(port));
   14147:	0f b7 45 ec          	movzwl -0x14(%ebp),%eax
   1414b:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   1414d:	ec                   	in     (%dx),%al
   1414e:	88 45 ff             	mov    %al,-0x1(%ebp)
	return rv;
   14151:	0f b6 45 ff          	movzbl -0x1(%ebp),%eax
}
   14155:	c9                   	leave  
   14156:	c3                   	ret

   14160:	66 89 45 ec          	mov    %ax,-0x14(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("in %1, %0" : "=a" (rv) : "dN" (port));
   14164:	0f b7 45 ec          	movzwl -0x14(%ebp),%eax

/**
 * @brief 等待磁盘有数据到达
 */
static inline int ata_wait_data (disk_t * disk) {
   14386:	55                   	push   %ebp
   14387:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   14389:	83 ec 10             	sub    $0x10,%esp
    uint8_t status;
	do {
        // 等待数据或者有错误
        status = inb(DISK_STATUS(disk));
   1438c:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   1438f:	0f b7 40 24          	movzwl 0x24(%eax),%eax

   143a2:	88 45 ff             	mov    %al,-0x1(%ebp)
        if ((status & (DISK_STATUS_BUSY | DISK_STATUS_DRQ | DISK_STATUS_ERR))
   143a5:	0f b6 45 ff          	movzbl -0x1(%ebp),%eax
   143a9:	25 89 00 00 00       	and    $0x89,%eax
   143ae:	3d 80 00 00 00       	cmp    $0x80,%eax
   143b3:	75 02                	jne    143b7 <ata_wait_data+0x31>
        status = inb(DISK_STATUS(disk));
   143b5:	eb d5                	jmp    1438c <ata_wait_data+0x6>
                        != DISK_STATUS_BUSY) {
            break;
   143b7:	90                   	nop
        }
    }while (1);

    // 检查是否有错误
    return (status & DISK_STATUS_ERR) ? -1 : 0;

static inline uint8_t inb(uint16_t  port) {
   14bc4:	55                   	push   %ebp
   14bc5:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   14bc7:	83 ec 14             	sub    $0x14,%esp
   14bca:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   14bcd:	66 89 45 ec          	mov    %ax,-0x14(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("inb %[p], %[v]" : [v]"=a" (rv) : [p]"d"(port));
   14bd1:	0f b7 45 ec          	movzwl -0x14(%ebp),%eax
   14bd5:	89 c2                	mov    %eax,%edx
   14bd7:	ec                   	in     (%dx),%al
   14bd8:	88 45 ff             	mov    %al,-0x1(%ebp)
	return rv;
   14bdb:	0f b6 45 ff          	movzbl -0x1(%ebp),%eax
}

   14be0:	c3                   	ret

/**

   14f2b:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp

   14f36:	0f b6 45 ec          	movzbl -0x14(%ebp),%eax
   14f3a:	50                   	push   %eax
   14f3b:	e8 c0 fc ff ff       	call   14c00 <get_key>

            break;

            break;

/**
 * @brief 按键中断处理程序
 */
void do_handler_kbd(exception_frame_t *frame) {

   14fb5:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   14fb7:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp

		BEGIN_E1,			// 收到e1字符

	// 检查是否有数据，无数据则退出

   14fc1:	83 c4 04             	add    $0x4,%esp

	if (!(status & KBD_STAT_RECV_READY)) {

   14fcb:	83 e0 01             	and    $0x1,%eax

   14fd0:	75 12                	jne    14fe4 <do_handler_kbd+0x30>

		return;
   14fdf:	e9 90 00 00 00       	jmp    15074 <do_handler_kbd+0xc0>

    uint8_t raw_code = inb(KBD_PORT_DATA);
   14fe4:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   14fe7:	6a 60                	push   $0x60
   14fe9:	e8 d6 fb ff ff       	call   14bc4 <inb>

	// 否则,键值的处理过程可能略长，将导致中断响应延迟

static inline void outb(uint16_t port, uint8_t data) {
   150b6:	55                   	push   %ebp
   150b7:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   150b9:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp
   150bc:	8b 55 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%edx
   150bf:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   150c2:	66 89 55 fc          	mov    %dx,-0x4(%ebp)
   150c6:	88 45 f8             	mov    %al,-0x8(%ebp)
	__asm__ __volatile__("outb %[v], %[p]" : : [p]"d" (port), [v]"a" (data));
   150c9:	0f b7 55 fc          	movzwl -0x4(%ebp),%edx
   150cd:	0f b6 45 f8          	movzbl -0x8(%ebp),%eax
   150d1:	ee                   	out    %al,(%dx)
}

static uint32_t sys_tick;						// 系统启动后的tick数量

/**
 * 定时器中断处理函数
 */
void do_handler_timer (exception_frame_t *frame) {
   150d5:	55                   	push   %ebp
   150d6:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   150d8:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp
    sys_tick++;
   150db:	a1 c4 65 03 00       	mov    0x365c4,%eax
   150e0:	83 c0 01             	add    $0x1,%eax
   150e3:	a3 c4 65 03 00       	mov    %eax,0x365c4

    // 先发EOI，而不是放在最后
    // 放最后将从任务中切换出去之后，除非任务再切换回来才能继续噢应
    pic_send_eoi(IRQ0_TIMER);
   150e8:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   150eb:	6a 20                	push   $0x20
   150ed:	e8 e4 dc ff ff       	call   12dd6 <pic_send_eoi>
   150f2:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp

    task_time_tick();
   150f5:	e8 65 c7 ff ff       	call   1185f <task_time_tick>
}

   150fc:	c3                   	ret

/**
 * 初始化硬件定时器
 */
static void init_pit (void) {
   150fd:	55                   	push   %ebp
   150fe:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   15100:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
    uint32_t reload_count = PIT_OSC_FREQ / (1000.0 / OS_TICK_MS);
   15103:	c7 45 f4 9b 2e 00 00 	movl   $0x2e9b,-0xc(%ebp)

    outb(PIT_COMMAND_MODE_PORT, PIT_CHANNLE0 | PIT_LOAD_LOHI | PIT_MODE0);
   1510a:	6a 36                	push   $0x36
   1510c:	6a 43                	push   $0x43
   1510e:	e8 a3 ff ff ff       	call   150b6 <outb>
   15113:	83 c4 08             	add    $0x8,%esp
    outb(PIT_CHANNEL0_DATA_PORT, reload_count & 0xFF);   // 加载低8位
   15116:	8b 45 f4             	mov    -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   15119:	0f b6 c0             	movzbl %al,%eax
   1511c:	50                   	push   %eax
   1511d:	6a 40                	push   $0x40
   1511f:	e8 92 ff ff ff       	call   150b6 <outb>
   15124:	83 c4 08             	add    $0x8,%esp
    outb(PIT_CHANNEL0_DATA_PORT, (reload_count >> 8) & 0xFF); // 再加载高8位
   15127:	8b 45 f4             	mov    -0xc(%ebp),%eax
   1512a:	c1 e8 08             	shr    $0x8,%eax
   1512d:	0f b6 c0             	movzbl %al,%eax
   15130:	50                   	push   %eax
   15131:	6a 40                	push   $0x40
   15133:	e8 7e ff ff ff       	call   150b6 <outb>
   15138:	83 c4 08             	add    $0x8,%esp

    irq_install(IRQ0_TIMER, (irq_handler_t)exception_handler_timer);

   1513e:	68 86 02 01 00       	push   $0x10286

/**
 * @brief 转换文件名为diritem中的短文件名，如a.txt 转换成a      txt
 */
static void to_sfn(char* dest, const char* src) {
   15d97:	55                   	push   %ebp
   15d98:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   15d9a:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp

   15da0:	6a 0b                	push   $0xb

   15da7:	e8 e9 26 00 00       	call   18495 <kernel_memset>
   15dac:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp

    // 不断生成直到遇到分隔符和写完缓存
    char * curr = dest;
   15daf:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   15db2:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)
    char * end = dest + SFN_LEN;
   15db5:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   15db8:	83 c0 0b             	add    $0xb,%eax
   15dbb:	89 45 ec             	mov    %eax,-0x14(%ebp)
    while (*src && (curr < end)) {
   15dbe:	eb 49                	jmp    15e09 <to_sfn+0x72>
        char c = *src++;
   15dc0:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   15dc3:	8d 50 01             	lea    0x1(%eax),%edx
   15dc6:	89 55 0c             	mov    %edx,0xc(%ebp)
   15dc9:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   15dcc:	88 45 f3             	mov    %al,-0xd(%ebp)

        switch (c) {
   15dcf:	0f be 45 f3          	movsbl -0xd(%ebp),%eax
   15dd3:	83 f8 2e             	cmp    $0x2e,%eax
   15dd6:	75 0b                	jne    15de3 <to_sfn+0x4c>
        case '.':       // 隔附，跳到扩展名区，不写字符
            curr = dest + 8;

 * 
 */
int sys_dup (int file) {
   175df:	55                   	push   %ebp
   175e0:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
   175e2:	83 ec 18             	sub    $0x18,%esp
	// 超出进程所能打开的全部，退出
	if (is_fd_bad(file)) { // file 小于 0 或大于“进程任务”可打开的文件表项数量，则认为参数 file 无效
   175e5:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   175e8:	e8 1d fa ff ff       	call   1700a <is_fd_bad>
   175ed:	83 c4 04             	add    $0x4,%esp
   175f0:	85 c0                	test   %eax,%eax
   175f2:	74 1a                	je     1760e <sys_dup+0x2f>
        log_printf("file(%d) is not valid.", file);
   175f4:	83 ec 08             	sub    $0x8,%esp
   175f7:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   175fa:	68 56 9d 01 00       	push   $0x19d56
   175ff:	e8 3b 14 00 00       	call   18a3f <log_printf>
   17604:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
		return -1;
   17607:	b8 ff ff ff ff       	mov    $0xffffffff,%eax
   1760c:	eb 6d                	jmp    1767b <sys_dup+0x9c>
	}

	file_t * p_file = task_file(file);  // 获取进程打开文件表file对应的表项,里面存储的是全局文件表的地址
   1760e:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   17611:	ff 75 08             	pushl  0x8(%ebp)
   17614:	e8 fd a0 ff ff       	call   11716 <task_file>
   17619:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
   1761c:	89 45 f4             	mov    %eax,-0xc(%ebp)
	if (!p_file) {
   1761f:	83 7d f4 00          	cmpl   $0x0,-0xc(%ebp)
   17623:	75 17                	jne    1763c <sys_dup+0x5d>
		log_printf("file not opened");
   17625:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   17628:	68 6d 9d 01 00       	push   $0x19d6d
   1762d:	e8 0d 14 00 00       	call   18a3f <log_printf>
   17632:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
		return -1;
   17635:	b8 ff ff ff ff       	mov    $0xffffffff,%eax
   1763a:	eb 3f                	jmp    1767b <sys_dup+0x9c>
	}

	int fd = task_alloc_fd(p_file);	// 新fd指向同一描述符
   1763c:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   1763f:	ff 75 f4             	pushl  -0xc(%ebp)
   17642:	e8 01 a1 ff ff       	call   11748 <task_alloc_fd>
   17647:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
   1764a:	89 45 f0             	mov    %eax,-0x10(%ebp)
	if (fd >= 0) {
   1764d:	83 7d f0 00          	cmpl   $0x0,-0x10(%ebp)
   17651:	78 13                	js     17666 <sys_dup+0x87>
		file_inc_ref(p_file);
   17653:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   17656:	ff 75 f4             	pushl  -0xc(%ebp)
   17659:	e8 2f f9 ff ff       	call   16f8d <file_inc_ref>
   1765e:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
		return fd;
   17661:	8b 45 f0             	mov    -0x10(%ebp),%eax
   17664:	eb 15                	jmp    1767b <sys_dup+0x9c>
	}

	log_printf("No task file avaliable");
   17666:	83 ec 0c             	sub    $0xc,%esp
   17669:	68 7d 9d 01 00       	push   $0x19d7d
   1766e:	e8 cc 13 00 00       	call   18a3f <log_printf>
   17673:	83 c4 10             	add    $0x10,%esp
    return -1;
   17676:	b8 ff ff ff ff       	mov    $0xffffffff,%eax
}
   1767b:	c9                   	leave  
   1767c:	c3                   	ret

   176c6:	e8 3c fd ff ff       	call   17407 <fs_protect>

 */

/**
 * @brief 移至第一个进程运行
 */

    // 注意，运行下面的代码可能会产生异常：段保护异常或页保护异常。
    // 可根据产生的异常类型和错误码，并结合手册来找到问题所在
    task_t * curr = task_current();

   17ca3:	e8 3a 0b 00 00       	call   187e2 <panic>

    tss_t * tss = &(curr->tss);

   17cb3:	89 45 f0             	mov    %eax,-0x10(%ebp)
        "push %[esp]\n\t"			// ESP
        "push %[eflags]\n\t"           // EFLAGS
        "push %[cs]\n\t"			// CS
        "push %[eip]\n\t"		    // ip

/**
 * 比较两个字符串，最多比较size个字符
 * 如果某一字符串提前比较完成，也算相同
 */
int kernel_strncmp (const char * s1, const char * s2, int size) {
   183cc:	55                   	push   %ebp
   183cd:	89 e5                	mov    %esp,%ebp
    if (!s1 || !s2) {
   183cf:	83 7d 08 00          	cmpl   $0x0,0x8(%ebp)
   183d3:	74 06                	je     183db <kernel_strncmp+0xf>
   183d5:	83 7d 0c 00          	cmpl   $0x0,0xc(%ebp)

        return -1;
   183db:	b8 ff ff ff ff       	mov    $0xffffffff,%eax
   183e0:	eb 62                	jmp    18444 <kernel_strncmp+0x78>
    }

    while (*s1 && *s2 && (*s1 == *s2) && size) {
    	s1++;
   183e2:	83 45 08 01          	addl   $0x1,0x8(%ebp)
    	s2++;
   183e6:	83 45 0c 01          	addl   $0x1,0xc(%ebp)
    while (*s1 && *s2 && (*s1 == *s2) && size) {
   183ea:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   183ed:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   183f0:	84 c0                	test   %al,%al
   183f2:	74 20                	je     18414 <kernel_strncmp+0x48>
   183f4:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   183f7:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   183fa:	84 c0                	test   %al,%al
   183fc:	74 16                	je     18414 <kernel_strncmp+0x48>
   183fe:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   18401:	0f b6 10             	movzbl (%eax),%edx
   18404:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   18407:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   1840a:	38 c2                	cmp    %al,%dl
   1840c:	75 06                	jne    18414 <kernel_strncmp+0x48>
   1840e:	83 7d 10 00          	cmpl   $0x0,0x10(%ebp)
   18412:	75 ce                	jne    183e2 <kernel_strncmp+0x16>
    }

    return !((*s1 == '\0') || (*s2 == '\0') || (*s1 == *s2));
   18414:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   18417:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   1841a:	84 c0                	test   %al,%al

   18421:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   18424:	84 c0                	test   %al,%al
   18426:	74 17                	je     1843f <kernel_strncmp+0x73>
   18428:	8b 45 08             	mov    0x8(%ebp),%eax
   1842b:	0f b6 10             	movzbl (%eax),%edx
   1842e:	8b 45 0c             	mov    0xc(%ebp),%eax
   18431:	0f b6 00             	movzbl (%eax),%eax
   18434:	38 c2                	cmp    %al,%dl
